================================================================================
DATA DICTIONARY REFERENCE GUIDE
================================================================================

This document provides descriptions of all data tables and their fields.
Use this as a reference to understand what data is available and how to use it.

================================================================================

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: APCheckDetail_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: AP Check Detail - Line-item details for AP checks.
FIELD COUNT: 3

FIELDS:
  - CheckNumber: Check Number
  - HostItemID: Check Number*seq
  - InvoiceNumber: Invoice Number (can be multiple paid per check)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: APCheck_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: AP Checks - Check payment records. Use for payment tracking and reconciliation.
FIELD COUNT: 11

FIELDS:
  - AccountNumber: Cash-in-bank Account Number
  - CheckAmount: Check Amount
  - CheckDate: Check Date
  - CheckNo: Check Number
  - CheckSource: Type
  - CompanyID: Cash Disbursement Journal Company from OPEN-AP.
  - DiscountAmount: Discount Amount
  - HostItemID: PICK item ID used by dataextractor for error reporting
  - PostFlag: Post Flag, 1 = posted
  - VendorNumber: Vendor Number
  - VoidFlag: Void Flag, V = void

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: APInvoiceDetail_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: AP Invoice Detail - Line-item details for AP invoices.
FIELD COUNT: 18

FIELDS:
  - AccountNumber: Account Number for the posting
  - CompanyID: Company number for the AccountNumber
  - Control: Control for the posting line if any
  - Control2: Control 2 for the posting line if any
  - EntryDate: Date of last entry or update
  - HostItemID: Vendor*Invoice*seq
  - InvoiceNumber: Invoice Number from Item ID
  - Journal: Journal posted to
  - JournalCompanyID: Journal Company Number
  - JournalDescription: Journal Description
  - PostFlag: 0=PostedAmount was posted, V=PostedAmount was voided
  - PostedAmount: Amount Posted without any discount
  - PostedDate: Date Amount was posted
  - PostingDescription: GL Account Posting Description
  - Productivity: Productivity Employee Number (type 7 or 8 from NAME-FILE)
  - SequenceNo: Schedules for Account if multiple (sep by \)
  - StatCount: Stat Count; could be null
  - VendorNumber: Vendor Number (without 2* prefix)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: APInvoice_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: AP Invoices - Vendor invoice records. Use for payables analysis and aging.
FIELD COUNT: 14

FIELDS:
  - CheckNumber: Check Number
  - DiscountAmount: Discount Amount
  - DsdaGuid: DSDA GUID
  - DueDate: Due date
  - HoldFlag: Hold flag
  - HostItemID: PICK item ID used by dataextractor for error reporting
  - InvoiceAmount: Invoice Amount
  - InvoiceComments: Invoice Comments
  - InvoiceDate: Invoice Date
  - InvoiceNumber: Invoice Number
  - PONumber: Purchase order number
  - VendorNumber: Vendor Number
  - YoozApprover: Yooz Approver
  - YoozDocId: Yooz Doc Id

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: ARAgingDetail_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: AR Aging Detail - Detailed aging of receivables. Use for collections analysis.
FIELD COUNT: 22

FIELDS:
  - AccountNumber: GL account number
  - CompanyID: GL company ID
  - CreditLimit: Customer's credit limit
  - CurrentDue: Balance owed for the current accounting month
  - CustNo: Customer control number
  - DeleteDataDate: CCPA Delete Data Date
  - DeleteDataFlag: CCPA Delete Data Flag
  - DeleteDataTime: CCPA Delete Data Time
  - ErrorLevel: ErrorLevel Flag
  - ErrorMessage: Error Message
  - HostItemID: PICK file item-id
  - Name1: Name1, stored as last name, first name
  - OptOutDate: CCPA Opt Out Date
  - OptOutFlag: CCPA Opt Out Flag
  - OptOutTime: CCPA Opt Out Time
  - Over120Due: Balance owed, aged over 120 days
  - Over30Due: Balance owed, aged between 30 and 59 days
  - Over60Due: Balance owed, aged between 60 and 89 days
  - Over90Due: Balance owed, aged between 90 and 119 days
  - PostAhead: Postahead amount
  - PreferredContact: Method of contact the customer prefers
  - Unposted: Unposted amount

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: ARBal_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: AR Balances - Customer account balances.
FIELD COUNT: 16

FIELDS:
  - ARAccountNumber: A/R Account Number
  - ARDate: Accounting date or last AR close
  - Control2: Control2 if present
  - Current: Current Amount Due
  - CustomerNumber: Customer Number
  - HostItemID: CustomerNumber*Seq
  - NameCode: Name Code Type, always = 4
  - Over120: If BF in attr 1 then over 120 days, If attribute 1 = null then credit entries.
  - Over30: If BF in attr 1 then 31 - 60 days, If attribute 1 = null then credit entries.
  - Over60: If BF in attr 1 then 61 - 90 days, If attribute 1 = null then credit entries.
  - Over90: If BF in attr 1 then 91 - 120 days, If attribute 1 = null then credit entries.
  - RecordType: Record Type, null = current month, BF = Balance Forward
  - Reference: Accounting Reference
  - ScheduleCode: Schedule Code
  - SourceJournal: Source Journal
  - TotalIntDue: Total Interest Due, Unpaid interest

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: ARComments_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: ARComments - Data table containing ARComments related information.
FIELD COUNT: 4

FIELDS:
  - Comment: Comment
  - CommentDate: Date of comment
  - CommentID: ID of comment / 1-100
  - HostItemID: AR Comment record ID - Customer Number

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: ARCustomerDetail_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: AR Customer Detail - Detailed customer AR information.
FIELD COUNT: 57

FIELDS:
  - AccountingDate: Accounting document date
  - CommentCounts: Customer comment counts from all comment files
  - CompanyID: Source Company ID
  - CreditLimit: Customer's credit limit
  - CreditMemoFlag: Credit Memo Flag
  - CreditMemoPrintFlag: Credit Memo Print Flag
  - CurrentDue: Balance owed for the current accounting month
  - CurrentMonth: GL Date of first day of the current month
  - CustNo: Customer Number
  - CustomerAddress: Street number and street name
  - CustomerAddress2: Second address line
  - CustomerCity: City
  - CustomerName: Name1, stored as last name, first name
  - CustomerName2: Name2, stored as last name, first name
  - CustomerState: Two-character state or province abbreviation
  - CustomerZipOrPostalCode: ZIP or postal code
  - DateAdded: Date that the control number was added to host.
  - DeleteDataDate: CCPA Delete Data Date
  - DeleteDataFlag: CCPA Delete Data Flag
  - DeleteDataTime: CCPA Delete Data Time
  - EmailAddress: Pipe Delimited list of customer email addresses
  - EmailDesc: Pipe Delimited list of customer email descriptions (correlative to EmailAddress)
  - FinanceCharge: Finance Charge
  - HostItemID: DMS PICK Record ID * Sequence Number
  - Interest: Lowest age at which interest is charged.
  - LastPayAmount: Amount of last payment
  - LastPmtDate: Last payment date
  - LastPurchAmount: Amount of last purchase
  - LastPurchDate: Last purchase date
  - NotYetInAccounting: Not yet in accounting
  - OptOutDate: CCPA Opt Out Date
  - OptOutFlag: CCPA Opt Out Flag
  - OptOutTime: CCPA Opt Out Time
  - Over120Due: Balance owed, aged over 120 days
  - Over30Due: Balance owed, aged between 30 and 59 days
  - Over60Due: Balance owed, aged between 60 and 89 days
  - Over90Due: Balance owed, aged between 90 and 119 days
  - PhoneDesc: Pipe Delimited list of phone descriptions (correlative to PhoneNumber)
  - PhoneExt: Pipe Delimited list of phone extensions (correlative to PhoneNumber). Only used for Business (extension) and Pager (access code).
  - PhoneNumber: Pipe Delimited list of phone numbers. Main, Home, Home FAX, Business, Business FAX, Cellular, Pager, Contact, Insurance Agent.
  - PostAheadAmount: Post Ahead amount
  - PostingAmount: Amount posted
  - PreferredContact: Method of contact the customer prefers
  - Profile: Profile, dealer defined grouping code
  - Refer: GL document reference number
  - ScheduleType: GL schedule type, B=AR-BAL (Sched A-M), O=AR-OPEN (Sched N-Y)
  - SrcJrnlID: GL source journal ID
  - StatementCurrentDue: Balance owed for the current accounting month
  - StatementDate: Last Statement date
  - StatementOver120Due: Balance owed, aged over 120 days
  - StatementOver30Due: Balance owed, aged between 30 and 59 days
  - StatementOver60Due: Balance owed, aged between 60 and 89 days
  - StatementOver90Due: Balance owed, aged between 90 and 119 days
  - YTDPurchases: Year-to-date purchases
  - Year1Amounts: Current Year month balances, <BR> delimited
  - Year2Amounts: One Year prior month balances, <BR> delimited
  - Year3Amounts: Two Years prior month balances, <BR> delimited

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: AROpenDetail_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: AR Open Detail - Open/unpaid AR items.
FIELD COUNT: 15

FIELDS:
  - ARAccountNumber: A/R Account Number
  - ARCompany: A/R Company Number
  - Amount: Invoice or Credit Amount
  - Control2: Control2 if present
  - CustomerNumber: Customer Number
  - HoldFlag: H=Hold reference from mulitiple posting option
  - HostItemID: ScheduleCode*CustomerNumber*InvoiceNumber*Seq
  - InvoiceNumber: Invoice Number from Item ID
  - JournalType: S=Sales Journal; R=Receipt Journal
  - Reference: Accounting Reference for the debit or credit
  - ReferenceDate: Reference Date for the invoice debit or credit
  - SaleCompany: Sale Company Number
  - ScheduleCode: Schedule Code
  - SourceJournal: Source Journal
  - TargetJournalCompany: Company number for the Target Journal

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: Ac1099Purchases_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: 1099 Purchases - 1099 reportable purchase data.
FIELD COUNT: 43

FIELDS:
  - AccountNumber: Account number if there are multiple accounts if more than one FORM 1099-MISC
  - Address: Vendor Address
  - Address2: Address2 from NAME-FILE
  - AttorneyProceeds: Amount of Attorney gross Proceeds, box 14.
  - City: Vendor City
  - Compensation: Amount of non-employee compensation paid, box 7
  - ControlType: Control Type, also known as Name Code, Always 2
  - CropProceeds: Crop insurance proceeds, box 10
  - DirectSales: Payer made directed sales of $5000.00 or more for resale, box 9
  - FedTaxWithheld: Amount of Federal income Tax Withheld, box 4
  - FederalTaxID: Federal Tax ID from NAME-FILE, taxpayer identification number (TIN), without dashes
  - FishingProceeds: Fishing boat proceeds, box 5
  - HostItemID: PICK File Item ID
  - Last4SSN: Last 4 of the SOCIAL SECURITY number
  - MedicalPaid: Amount of Medical Payments paid, box 6
  - Name2: Name 2 from NAME-FILE
  - Other: Other income, box 3
  - ParachutePayments: Amount of excess Parachute Payments, box 13.
  - PrintFlag: Print 1099-MISC form, 1099.FLAG from NAME-FILE, 1, 0, or null
  - RecordCode: Record Code. G, GX, C, O or null
  - Rent: Amount of rents paid, box 1
  - ReportYear: Year of Purchase
  - Royalties: Amount of royalties paid, box 2
  - Sec409ADeferrals: Section 409A deferrals, box 15a
  - Sec409AIncome: Section 409A Income, box 15b
  - State: Vendor State
  - StateCode1: First state code, box 17. Correlative to field 29
  - StateCode2: Second state code, box 17. Correlative to field 30
  - StateID1: First state taxpayer ID, box 17. Correlative to field 35
  - StateID2: Second state taxpayer ID, box 17. Correlative to field 36
  - StateIncome1: State 1 Income, box 18
  - StateIncome2: State 2 income, box 18
  - StateTaxWithheld1: State Tax Withheld, box 16
  - StateTaxWithheld2: Second State Withholding Tax amt, box 16
  - SubstitutePayments: Amount of Substitute Payments in lieu of dividends or interest, box 8
  - TimeStamp: Date/time stamp
  - TinNotice: Second TIN Notice indicator
  - TypeFlag: Type flag of record. Alpha character G, C, GX, O, or null
  - UserName: User name
  - VendorName: Vendor Name
  - VendorNumber: Vendor Number
  - YTDPurchases: YTD-PURCH amt from NAME-FILE
  - ZipCode: ZIP Code, 5 or 10-digit zip code with the dash (-), 97233-4042

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: AppointmentsDetail_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: Appointments Detail - Service appointment details.
FIELD COUNT: 24

FIELDS:
  - ApptID: Appointment ID
  - ComeBack: Indicates if this is a comeback Y/N
  - ComebackRO: The original repair order number
  - ComebackSA: The original service advisor's number
  - ComebackTech: The original technician's number
  - ComplaintCode: Complaint code number
  - Cost: Labor operation cost
  - Date: Appointment date
  - EstimatedDuration: Estimated Duration of the technician's work time, in hours
  - HostItemID: Labor ops ID
  - LaborType: Labor type for the labor operation
  - LineCode: Line to which this labor operation applies
  - LineConcernCode: Concern Codes on lines
  - LineDispatchCode: Dispatch Codes on lines (if appropriate)
  - OpCode: Op Code for this labor operation
  - OpCodeDesc: Description of this labor operation
  - Sale: Labor operation sale amount
  - SeqNo: 
  - ServiceDesc: Description of this labor operation
  - ServiceRequest: Service requests.
  - SoldHours: Hours sold for this labor operation
  - TechNo: Technician number assigned to the labor operation
  - linServiceEstimate: Total service estimate for the service request (line).
  - linTechnician: Technician number for the service request (line)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: Appointments_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: Appointments - Data table containing Appointments related information.
FIELD COUNT: 79

FIELDS:
  - Address2: Address line 2
  - AppointmentDate: Appointment Date
  - AppointmentTime: Appointment Time
  - ApptAddress: Customer Address
  - ApptCityStateZip: Customer City, State, ZIP or Postal Code
  - ApptContactEmail: Contact Email Address
  - ApptContactPhone: Contact Phone Number
  - ApptCustName: Customer Name
  - ApptDate: Appointment Date
  - ApptID: Appointment ID
  - ApptMileage: Mileage
  - ApptName: Customer Name
  - ApptOpenDate: Appointment Open Date
  - ApptOpenTime: Appointment Open Time
  - ApptTime: Appointment Time
  - BusinessPhone: Customer's business phone
  - BusinessPhoneExt: Customer's business phone extension
  - Cellular: Cell phone number
  - Color: Exterior color
  - Comments: Comments.
  - ComplaintSummary: Complaint Summary
  - CustNo: Customer Number
  - DELETEPIIDATA: Customer marked their PII as deleted
  - DropOffCity: Shuttle Drop Off City
  - DropOffDate: Shuttle Drop Off Date
  - DropOffNote: Shuttle Drop Off Note
  - DropOffPhoExt: Shuttle Drop Off Phone Ext
  - DropOffPhone: Shuttle Drop Off Phone
  - DropOffTime: Shuttle Drop Off Time
  - DropOffVanNo: Shuttle Drop Off Van No
  - DropOffaAddr: Shuttle Drop Off Addr
  - EMail: Email address.
  - EstCompDate: Estimated Completion Date
  - EstCompTime: Estimated Completion Time
  - FirstName: Customer First Name
  - HomePhone: Home telephone number
  - HostItemID: Appointment ID
  - LastName: Customer Last Name
  - Make: Full name of vehicle.
  - MakeAbbr: Make Abbreviation
  - MiddleName: Customer Middle Name
  - Model: Full name of model.
  - ModelAbbr: Model Abbreviation
  - ModelYear: Model Year
  - NoShowFlag: No-show flag (0/1) set if appointment was not kept.
  - OPTOUTSELLINGPIIDATA: Customer has blocked the selling of their PII
  - OPTOUTSHARINGPIIDATA: Customer has blocked the sharing of their PII
  - OriginAppl: Application that initially created the appointment.
  - OriginCode: Code indicating the type of transaction from a third-party application.
  - PickUpCity: Shuttle Pick Up City
  - PickUpDate: Shuttle Pick Up Date
  - PickUpNote: Shuttle Pick Up Note
  - PickUpPhoExt: Shuttle Pick Up Phone Ext
  - PickUpPhone: Shuttle Pick Up Phone
  - PickUpTime: Shuttle Pick Up Time
  - PickUpVanNo: Shuttle Pick Up Van No
  - PickUpaAddr: Shuttle Pick Up Addr
  - PromiseDate: Promise Date
  - PromiseTime: Promise Time
  - Remarks: Remarks entered at appointment writeup.
  - Reservationist: Reservationist number.
  - SAName: Service Advisor Name
  - SANumber: Service Advisor Number
  - SalesPerson: Primary Salespersons name.
  - SalesPersonID: Primary Salespersons ID
  - ServiceLaneType: GM Service Lane Type - EXPRESS_SERVICE OR DEFAULT
  - StockNo: Vehicle's stock number
  - StockType: Stock type
  - TotalDuration: Total estimated duration for the appointment.
  - TransType: Alternate transportation code.
  - TrimLevel: Trim Level
  - VIN: Vehicle Identification
  - Vehid: Vehicle ID
  - VehidOrCust: Vehid or Customer Number
  - WaiterFlag: Waiter flag (0/1) set if customer will wait for repairs.
  - estRoServiceTotal: Current service total estimate amount
  - estRoTotal: Current total estimate for the repair order
  - nofModel: Vehicle model abbreviation for an APPT appointment (vehicle not on file on the DMS).
  - nofYear: Vehicle model year for an APPT appointment (vehicle not on file on the DMS).

  - HostItemID: Check Number*seq

  - VendorNumber: Vendor Number
  - VoidFlag: Void Flag, V = void

TABLE: BuODCCheckDetail_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: Business Unit ODC Check Detail - ODC checks by business unit.
FIELD COUNT: 15

FIELDS:
  - AStat: Name: AStat, Desc: AStat
  - AcctDescription: Name: A-DESC, Desc: A-DESC
  - Aprod: Name: AProd, Desc: AProd
  - CheckNo: Name: ID, Desc: Check Number
  - Control1: Name: A-CNTL, Desc: A-CNTL
  - Control2: Name: A-CNTL2, Desc: A-CNTL2
  - GLAccount: Name: GLAccount, Desc: GL Account
  - GLAmount: Name: A-AMT, Desc: Amount posted to GLAccount
  - HostItemID: Name: HostItemID, Desc: DMS File Item ID * MV Sequence
  - Jrnl: Name: Jrnl, Desc: Jrnl
  - JrnlCo: Name: JrnlCo, Desc: JrnlCo

  - UserID: Name: USER-ID, Desc: USER-ID
  - UserName: Name: USER-ID, Desc: USER-ID

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: BuODCInvoiceDetail_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: Business Unit ODC Invoice Detail - ODC invoices by business unit.
FIELD COUNT: 10

FIELDS:
  - CheckNo: Name: ID, Desc: Check Number
  - HostItemID: Name: HostItemID, Desc: DMS File Item ID * MV Sequence
  - InvCommentorVIN: Name: COMMENT-VIN#, Invoice comment or vehicle identification number. (Multivalued and correlative to attributes 7-11.)
  - InvCommentorVIN2: Name: COMMENT-VIN#, Invoice comment or vehicle identification number. (Multivalued and correlative to attributes 7-11.)
  - InvoiceAmount: Name: I-AMOUNT, Invoice amounts. (Multivalued and correlative to attributes 7, 8, and 10-12.)
  - InvoiceDate: Name: I-DATE, Invoice dates in internal format. (Multivalued and correlative to attributes 7, and 9-12.)
  - InvoiceDiscount: Name: I-DISCOUNT, Invoice discount amounts. (Multivalued and correlative to attributes 7-9, 11, and 12.)
  - InvoiceNo: Name: INVOICE, Desc: Invoice numbers. (Multivalued and correlative to attributes 8-12.)
  - PurOrdorStockNo: Name: P/O-STK, Purchase order or stock number. (Multivalued and correlative to attributes 7-10, and 12.)
  - VendorOrCustNo: Name: PAYEE

TABLE: BuODCRegister_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: BuODCRegister - Data table containing BuODCRegister related information.
FIELD COUNT: 35

FIELDS:
  - AcctCoVoided: Account company for void
  - AcctNoVoided: Account number for void
  - AmtVoided: Amount voided for AcctNoVoided
  - CheckAmount: Name: C-AMOUNT, Desc: CHK-AMT
  - CheckDate: Name: C-DATE, Desc: CHECK DATE
  - CheckNo: Name: ID, Desc: Check Number
  - CheckType: Name: C-TYPE
  - CompanyCode: Name: Company Code, Desc: Company Code
  - Control2Voided: Control 2 Void Original chk entries
  - ControlVoided: Control number for AcctNoVoided
  - CreatedByID: Name: USER-ID, Desc: USER-ID
  - CreatedByName: Name: USER-ID, Desc: USER-ID
  - HostItemID: Name: HostItemID, Desc: DMS File Item ID
  - JrnlCoVoided: Journal company for void
  - JrnlDescVoided: Journal description for void
  - Name2: Name2 of payee, If Payee# and N-CD then NAME2 from NAME-FILE
  - NameCode: Name: NAME-CD, Desc: NAME-CD
  - Payee1099Flag: Name: 1099.FLAG, Desc: 1099.FLAG
  - PayeeAddress: Name: ADDRESS, Desc: ADDRESS
  - PayeeAddress2: Name: ADDRESS2, Desc: ADDRESS2
  - PayeeCity: Name: CITY, Desc: CITY
  - PayeeName: Name: NAME, Desc: NAME
  - PayeeNo: Name: PAYEE
  - PayeeState: Name: STATE, Desc: STATE
  - PayeeZip: Name: ZIP, Desc: ZIP
  - PostDescVoided: Posting description for void
  - ProdNoVoided: Productivity number for account for void
  - ReportFlag: Name: Report Flag, Desc: Report Flag
  - SoJrnlVoided: Source journal for void
  - StatCntVoided: Statistical count for void
  - VendorOrCustNo: Name: PAYEE
  - VoidDate: Name: Void Date, Desc: Void Date
  - VoidFlag: Name: VOID, Desc: V D
  - VoidedByID: Name: USER-ID, Desc: USER-ID
  - VoidedByName: Name: USER-ID, Desc: USER-ID

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: BusinessOfficeConsolidation_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: Business Office Consolidation - Business office consolidation data.
FIELD COUNT: 7

FIELDS:
  - AccountingAccount: AA, Accounting account name (source logon)
  - ControlNumber: CN, Control number before business office consolidation
  - ControlType: CT, Control Type (1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 7 or 8)
  - HostItemID: Host Item-ID (AA*CT*CN)
  - NewAccountingAccount: New accounting account name (target logon)
  - NewControlExistsFlag: New control exists in NAME-FILE (0=No, 1=Yes)
  - NewControlNumber: Control number after business office consolidation

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: CiCiffAuditDetails_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: CI CIFF Audit Details - CIFF audit detail records.
FIELD COUNT: 15

FIELDS:
  - Auto: Auto Post Flag
  - Date: Audit Dates
  - DealNo: Deal Number from record ID
  - ErrorDetails: Error Details
  - ErrorID: Error ID
  - ErrorText: Error Text
  - HostItemID: Logon*Deal#*Sequence*0
  - LastStat: Last Status
  - Logon: Logon from record ID
  - ProcUsed: Proc Name
  - Program: Program Routine which Modified the deal
  - Stat: Status
  - Time: Audit Times
  - UserId: User ID whom Modified the deal
  - VehStat: Vehicle Status

TABLE: CiraEIVOffset_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: CIRA EIV Offset - CIRA EIV offset records.
FIELD COUNT: 6

FIELDS:
  - CoreOffsetJrnlAmt: Core Interim Account Offset Journal Entry debit amount.
  - CoreOffsetJrnlID: Core Interim Account Offset Journal Entry item ID.
  - HostItemID: Part receiving number ~ Sequence Number.
  - PRNID: CiraEIV Table HostItemID - Part receiving number.
  - PartsOffsetJrnlAmt: Parts Interim Account Offset Journal Entry debit amount.
  - PartsOffsetJrnlID: Parts Interim Account Offset Journal Entry item ID.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: CiraEIVParts_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: CiraEIVParts - Data table containing CiraEIVParts related information.
FIELD COUNT: 6

FIELDS:

  - HostItemID: Part receiving number ~ Sequence Number.
  - PRNID: CiraEIV Table HostItemID - Part receiving number.
  - PartNbr: Part number.
  - PartsUnitCost: Parts unit cost.
  - Qty: Quantity.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: CiraEIV_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: CIRA EIV - CIRA electronic invoice verification.
FIELD COUNT: 18

FIELDS:
  - CoreClearedDate: Core interim account cleared" date."
  - CoreJrnlAmt: Core Interim Account Journal Entry credit amount.
  - CoreJrnlCntl2: Core Receiving Journal Entry Control 2" value."
  - CoreJrnlID: Core Interim Account Journal Entry item ID.
  - HostItemID: Pick file ItemID - Parts Receiving Number
  - OrderNbr: Parts order number.
  - PONbr: PO Number.
  - PRNID: PO Number.
  - PartsAcct: Parts Account where receipt was created and CRAE Accounting Interface setups exist.
  - PartsJrnlAmt: Parts Interim Account Journal Entry credit amount.
  - PartsJrnlCntl2: Parts Receiving Journal Entry Control 2" value."
  - PartsJrnlID: Parts Interim Account Journal Entry item ID.
  - PartsRcptNbr: Parts receiving number.
  - PosingID: CRAE Acct Interface Setups ID..
  - PtsClearedDate: Parts interim account cleared" date."
  - ReceivingDate: Receiving date.

TABLE: CoreRtnHistHdr_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: CoreRtnHistHdr - Data table containing CoreRtnHistHdr related information.
FIELD COUNT: 22

FIELDS:
  - BillLadingNbr: Freight carriers shipment identification (Bill of Lading) document number.
  - CreateDate: Date that the return was initially created.
  - DealerCode: The identifier assigned to the dealer by the vendor. Initially pulled from the vendor file.
  - HostItemID: Name: HostItemID, Desc: DMS File Item ID
  - LastModDate: Last date that the return was modified. Initial value in this field is the create date. Is changed every time the user makes a change to the open return.
  - ProcessDate: Date the return officially changed to shipped status. This is the date that the return information is copied from the working return files to the history files.
  - ReturnComment: Single line freeform comment containing information for processing this return.
  - RtnGdRefNbr: Vendor Return Goods Reference number.
  - ShipDate: Date when the return left the dealership and was sent to the vendor.
  - ShipLocation: Vendor location number.
  - ShipToAddr1: MV1 = Street Address #1. Address information pulled from vendor file (using location#).
  - ShipToAddr2: MV2 = Street Address #2. Address information pulled from vendor file (using location#).
  - ShipToCity: MV3 = City. City information pulled from vendor file (using location#).
  - ShipToStateProv: MV4 = State/Prov. State/Province information pulled from vendor file (using location#).
  - ShipToZip: MV5 = Zip. Zip information pulled from vendor file (using location#).
  - ShipVia: Name of the freight carrier selected for this return. Default is initially pulled from the Vendor file.
  - TotalItems: Number of unique part IDs.
  - TotalPieces: Number of pieces for all parts added together.
  - TotalValue: Total EXCHG value for the return; maximum return value. Stored without decimal point; displayed MD2.
  - TotalWeight: All the weights for all quantities added together.
  - VendorName: Name of the vendor that the dirty cores were returned to. Initially pulled from the vendor file.
  - VendorNbr: Item ID of record in IN.VENDORS file, this is a required field for all vendor returns.

FIELD COUNT: 26

FIELDS:

  - EstimateTime: Time. Contains the time of the original or revised estimate.

  - ServiceAdvisorNo: Service Advisor Number
  - ServiceEstimate: Service total estimate. Contains the total estimate for service charges.
  - ServiceLaborEstimate: Service labor subtotal estimate. Contains the labor subtotal estimate for service charges. This is a dollar amount: $100.00 stores as 10000.
  - ServiceLubeEstimate: Service lube subtotal estimate. Contains the lube subtotal estimate for service charges. This is a dollar amount: $100.00 stores as 10000.
  - ServiceMiscEstimate: Service miscellaneous subtotal estimate. Contains the miscellaneous subtotal estimate for service charges. This is a dollar amount: $100.00 stores as 10000.
  - ServicePartsEstimate: Service parts subtotal estimate. Contains the parts subtotal estimate for service charges. This is a dollar amount: $100.00 stores as 10000.
  - ServiceSubletEstimate: Service sublet subtotal estimate. Contains the sublet subtotal estimate for service charges. This is a dollar amount: $100.00 stores as 10000.
  - ServiceTaxEstimate: Service tax subtotal estimate. Contains the tax subtotal estimate for service charges. This is a dollar amount: $100.00 stores as 10000.
  - TotalEstimate: Total Estimated Amount
  - VehID: Vehicle ID. The vehicle identification this estimate is for (VEHICLES, attribute 0).

TABLE: DeniedWorkHistory_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: Denied Work History - History of declined service work.
FIELD COUNT: 24

FIELDS:
  - ClosedDate: Date the repair order was closed.
  - Comment: Denied work comments (for example phone number and/or additional comments. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - CustNo: Customer number on the repair order.
  - DELETEPIIDATA: Customer marked their PII as deleted
  - DenyCode: Denied Work Code from RO. Multivalue Key for each row. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - DenyContact: Name of the person that was contacted and denied the recommended work. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - DenyDate: Date the denied work was added to the appointment or repair order. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - DenyEmployeeNo: Employee number of who added the denied work. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - DenyReason: Reason work was denied by the customer. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - DenyTime: Time the denied work was added to the appointment or repair order. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - HostItemID: HostItemID - VEHID * RO * Mv * Sv
  - Name1: Using 4*CustNo to get the Name1 from NAME-FILE.
  - OPTOUTSELLINGPIIDATA: Customer has blocked the selling of their PII
  - OPTOUTSHARINGPIIDATA: Customer has blocked the sharing of their PII
  - RONumber: Repair Order Number (2nd position delimited by '*').
  - RecDate: Date work was recommended or requested. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - RecEmployeeNo: Employee number of who recommended the work. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - RecEstimate: Estimated cost of the recommended work. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - RecLineCode: Line code of the line associated with the recommended work. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - RecOpCode: Op Code of the recommended work that was denied. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - RecOpCodeDesc: Description of the recommended work that was denied. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - RecTime: Time work was recommended or requested. Correlative to HISTORY-LINES<11>.
  - ServiceAccount: Service Account from HISTORY / 12.
  - VehID: Vehicle Identification (1st position delimited by '*').

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: DiscountCodes_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: Discount Codes - Discount configuration and rules.
FIELD COUNT: 42

FIELDS:
  - AccountCP: Customer Pay company and account number option D or L. D = Use the discount setup; L = Use the labor type assigned (attribute 15)
  - AccountIP: Internal Pay company and account number option D or L. D = Use the discount setup; L = Use the labor type assigned (attribute 15)
  - AccountWP: Warranty Pay company and account number option D or L. D = Use the discount setup; L = Use the labor type assigned (attribute 15)
  - AllowDuplicate: Allow discount to be added more than once to an RO. Y=Yes; N or null=No
  - AllowOverride: Allow override of discount (amount; percent or target price). N or null=No; Y=Yes
  - Apply: Discount Application. Indicates if the discount calculation applies to labor sale and/or parts sale (L=labor; P=parts; B=both)
  - BeginDate: Begin Date
  - DiscountCode: Discount Code
  - DiscountDesc: Discount Description
  - DiscountMethod: Discount Method F=Fixed; P=Percent; T=Target Price
  - EndDate: End Date
  - FixedPrice: Fixed Amount. Only contains a value if discount method is fixed (F)
  - HostItemID: PICK file item ID
  - LaborAccount: Labor discount GL account number. Multivalued and correlative to Labor Parent Class (attribute 20). First if Multivalued
  - LaborClass: Labor parent class C; W; or I. C = Customer Pay; W = Warranty Pay; I = Internal Pay. First if Multivalued
  - LaborClassCP: Customer Pay Discount Allowed. Y=Discount can be applied to CP; N or null = Discount cannot be applied to CP
  - LaborClassIP: Internal Pay Discount Allowed. Y=Discount can be applied to IP; N or null = Discount cannot be applied to IP
  - LaborClassWP: Warranty Pay Discount Allowed. Y=Discount can be applied to WP; N or null = Discount cannot be applied to WP
  - LaborCompany: Labor discount target company. Multivalued and correlative to Labor Parent Class (attribute 20). First if Multivalued
  - LaborPercent: Percent of labor discount to be posted to GL account number. Multivalued and correlative to Labor Parent Class (attribute 20). First if Multivalued
  - LaborTypeCP: Discount labor type for CP. RO-MLS record labor type for Customer Pay
  - LaborTypeIP: Discount labor type for IP. RO-MLS record labor type for Internal Pay
  - LaborTypeWP: Discount labor type for WP. RO-MLS record labor type for Warranty Pay
  - MaxDiscount: Maximum discount amount. Only contains a value if discount method is percent (P) or target pricing (T)
  - MaxOverride: If discount can be override; the maximum amount of the override discount amount
  - MinProfitAmtCP: Minimum profitable amount for Customer Pay of parts and labor with the discount applied before a PFC warning message
  - MinProfitAmtIP: Minimum profitable amount for Internal Pay of parts and labor with the discount applied before a PFC warning message
  - MinProfitAmtWP: Minimum profitable amount for Warranty Pay of parts and labor with the discount applied before a PFC warning message
  - MinProfitPercCP: Minimum profitable percentage for Customer Pay of parts and labor with the discount applied before a PFC warning message
  - MinProfitPercIP: Minimum profitable percentage for Internal Pay of parts and labor with the discount applied before a PFC warning message
  - MinProfitPercWP: Minimum profitable percentage for Warranty Pay of parts and labor with the discount applied before a PFC warning message
  - PartsAccount: Parts discount GL account number. Multivalued and correlative to Parts Parent Class (attribute 24). First if Multivalued
  - PartsClass: Parts parent class C; W; or I. C = Customer Pay; W = Warranty Pay; I = Internal Pay. First if Multivalued
  - PartsCompany: Parts discount target company. Multivalued and correlative to Parts Parent Class (attribute 24). First if Multivalued
  - PartsPercent: Percent of parts discount to be posted to GL account number. Multivalued and correlative to Parts Parent Class (attribute 24). First if Multivalued
  - Percentage: Percent of labor and /or parts sale amounts. Only contains a value if discount method is percent (P)
  - Restricted: Indicates if the discount code is restricted. N or null=No; Y=Yes
  - SplitCP: Split discount by S = Sale amounts; G = Gross profit for Customer Pay
  - SplitIP: Split discount by S = Sale amounts; G = Gross profit for Internal Pay
  - SplitWP: Split discount by S = Sale amounts; G = Gross profit for Warranty Pay
  - TargetFrom: Use op code target price if op code has target price. Only valid if method is target price (T) D=Use discount setup; O=Use op code price
  - TargetPrice: Target price after discount applied. Only contains a value if discount method is target price (T)

TABLE: EtcTransHist_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: ETC Transaction History - Historical time clock transactions.
FIELD COUNT: 34

FIELDS:
  - AutoLunch: Will have Auto Lunch Deduct Overridden if used in TCA/O.
  - BreakClockInTime: Clock in time for attributes 28 - 32 if attribute 28 = Y.
  - BreakClockOut: Answer to question Are you clocking out for break? Y=Yes; N=No for attributes 29 - 32
  - BreakClockOutTime: Clock out time for attributes 28 - 32 if attribute 28 = Y.
  - BreakDuration: Duration of actual break. Numeric.
  - BreakPaid: Paid compensation (based on 1 break per 4 hours worked. Numeric.
  - ClockIn: Time the employee clocks in.
  - ClockMessage: Clock in or out error message reported by security & violation checks.
  - ClockMessageTime: Time the clock error message in attribute 10 was recorded.
  - ClockOut: Time the employee clocks out.
  - CompanyNumber: ETC Company Number
  - Duration: Duration, seconds between clock in and clock out.
  - EROHoursSold: Sold Hours from TECH-PAYROLL when ERO interface is used by TCA/EI, Numeric,200=2.0 hours.
  - EROHoursTechPaylIds: TECH-PAYROLL item-IDs where the sold hours in attribute 20 were found.
  - EROPayFlag: Flag to pay ERO employee for the hours posted through TCA/O. Y if true.
  - EmployeeNumber: ETC Employee Number
  - EtcDate: Date entered in ETC
  - HostItemID: PICK file item ID
  - LastEntryDate: This date is used for calculating the elapsed hours in attribute 3.
  - Newtime: New override time, as entered through TCA/O or TCA/MO.
  - OldTime: The old time before the override was done through TCA/O or TCA/MO
  - OverrideColumnDesc: Full Override description, correlative to attribute 15.
  - OverrideColumnType: Type of override done in attr 1 & 2. Used for ETC.TIMECARD for which column, V,H,S,T,A,O.
  - OverrideDate: System date when the override was done through TCA/O or TCA/MO.
  - OverrideDescription: The long text description of the override code contained in attribute 12.
  - OverrideEmployee: Employee number of the manager who did the override through TCA/O or TCA/MO.
  - OverrideMode: Override mode for the override done through TCA/O or TCA/MO, I-In, O-Out.
  - OverrideTime: System time when the override was done through TCA/O or TCA/MO.
  - OverrideType: Override type for the override done through TCA/O or TCA/MO, V=Vac H=Holi S=Sick T=Train A=Auth O=Other.
  - SecurityError: Security breach error message received, report not authorized, Invalid Pin, etc.
  - SecurityErrorTime: The internal time a security breach was recorded, correlative to attribute 17.
  - ServiceLogon: The Service account where the TECH-PAYROLL file was located
  - TimeZoneIn: Time zone for the employee's clock-in records if enabled in TCA/U/TZ. EDT, PST, etc.
  - TimeZoneOut: Time zone for the employee's clock-out records if enabled in TCA/U/TZ. EDT, PST, etc.

TABLE: FsCalculatedData_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: Financial Statement Calculated Data - Stores computed financial statement values and results.
FIELD COUNT: 12

FIELDS:
  - FormattedNumeric: Calculated results. Contains one of the following types of information:<P>Null if the TypeOfData field is 0 (literal value). Null if the account number balance is zero when the TypeOfData field is 1 (formatted numeric).<P>Number of units, repair orders, or contracts or dollar amount. The numeric string can contain a negative or parentheses if not the expected sign.<P>The numeric string can contain commas every three digits before the decimal.
  - FsColumn: The column number on the specified financial statement page.
  - FsLine: The line number on the specified financial statement page.
  - FsNumber: The financial statement number on this DMS.
  - FsOverFlow: If the length of the FormattedNumeric string exceeds the specified space on the financial statement, an overflow indicator is stored in the FsOverFlow field.<P>Each overflow indicator is a unique sequential letter from A to Z, and then two letter codes from AA to AZ, BA to BA, etc.<P>If the formatted number fits in the specified space on the financial statement, the formatted number is stored in FINAL-WORK-FILE-nbr <3> and the FsOverFlow field is set to null.
  - FsPage: The specified financial statement page.
  - HostItemID: The HostItemID is an ID generated by the EIP to uniquely identify how the record was generated.
  - LiteralValue: If the TypeOfData field is 0, then the field contains a literal value or null.<P>Null if the TypeOfData field is 1.
  - NumericValue: The numeric value of the FormattedNumeric value. The numeric value scale factor is the same as the Formatted Numeric string. A percentage value of 1234 can be scaled 100 times larger than the amount printed for the financial statement as 12.34%.
  - PeriodEndDate: The financial statement PeriodEndDate is the last day of the specified period (month and year).
  - PlcCode: The Financial Statement page, line, and column number code. (each field is in base 25)
  - TypeOfData: Indicates if the FormattedNumeric field is a formatted number (1) or a literal value (0).

  - DealershipCityStatePostalCode: Dealership city, state and postal code

TABLE: FsStatementStatus_v

DESCRIPTION: Financial Statement Status - Tracks status of financial statements.
FIELD COUNT: 15

FIELDS:

  - PeriodEndDate: The financial statement PeriodEndDate is the last day of the specified period (month and year).
  - StatementDate: The date entered by the user in FST to specify the financial statement calculation period. The user can enter any date in a month. Any date between 5/01/2002 and 5/31/2002, specifies to FST to calculate the financial statements for May, 2002.
  - TypeOfYear: Specifies the type of statement: calendar year or fiscal year statement.<P>C = calendar year.<BR>F = fiscal year.
  - UserID: The user ID of the person who marked the financial statement final.

TABLE: NameFileEvents_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: Name File Events - Events related to name file changes.
FIELD COUNT: 10

FIELDS:
  - Control: Control Number (dealer assigned)
  - EventDate: System date on which the event occurred.
  - EventTime: System time when the event occurred on the EventDate.
  - EventType: The type of event being tracked.<P>Attribute number = Change to that attribute. Which attributes are tracked is controlled by PRIVLIB TRACK-EVENTS.
  - HostItemID: PICK file item ID
  - Household: Indicates if there is a household change associated with the address change.
  - NameCode: Control type. See the GL.VALID file CNTL item.
  - NewData: Optional. Change records, only. The data after the change.
  - OldData: This contains the first value of a multivalued field. All values are available using the NameFileEventsOldData integration point.<P>Pending Delete and Deleted records - Contents of NAME-FILE <2> prior to the delete request.<P>Failed deletion records - Contents of NAME-FILE <2> prior to the delete request, plus additional values, one for each failure reason.
  - UserID: ID of the user making the addition, change, or deletion. (Processes run in Job-Stack like NT.MERGE.NAMES can record the user ID as 'jobstack'.)<P>If tracked data was modified from a Parts account (functions I and OCCU), the employee might have entered their employee number. If so, the value is 'P#nnnn', in place of their user.id, where 'nnnn' is the employee number.

TABLE: PartsInventory_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: Parts Inventory - Complete parts inventory with quantities, costs, pricing.
FIELD COUNT: 140

FIELDS:
  - ABCD: A.B.C.D. or informational field
  - ABCXYZ: Cost Ranking Code
  - AUOM: Acquisition unit of measure.Valid are :ea,bx,case,ctn,gal etc..
  - AccountingAccount: Associated accounting account
  - Appreciation: Net month-to-date change in value of part
  - AprSales: April demand history, current year
  - AprSales2: April demand history, last year
  - AprSales3: April demand history, two years ago
  - ArrivedFlag: Arrived flag
  - AugSales: August demand history, current year
  - AugSales2: August demand history, last year
  - AugSales3: August demand history, two years ago
  - AutoPhaseoutQualifiedMonths: No of months to look at to call for Auto Phaseout
  - AutomaticPhaseoutQualifier: No of sales below which a part can be called for AP
  - BOPCK: BOPCK Interchangeability code
  - BRP: Best reorder point
  - BSL: Best stocking level
  - BaseCostLIFO: Base cost for LIFO calculations
  - BegQtyLIFO: Beginning quantity for LIFO calculations
  - BestReorderPoint: No of days user want the stk maintained before an order is placed.
  - Bin1: First bin location
  - Bin2: Second bin location
  - Bin3: Third bin location
  - CURMTD: Current month to date.
  - Class: Classification code
  - Cntr: Transaction type counter
  - Comment: Client information applicable to the part
  - CommentFlag: Comment indicator
  - Comp: Wholesale compensation amount
  - CoreMatrix: Core Group/Matrix Number
  - CoreSerialized: Serialized Part indicator
  - Cost: Cost price or dealer net
  - DateAdded: Date of entry
  - DateLastReceipted: Date last receipted
  - DecSales: December demand history, current year
  - DecSales2: December demand history, last year
  - DecSales3: December demand history, two years ago
  - DeletePartFlag: Delete Part Flag
  - Description: Part number description
  - DirtyBin1: Bin 1 location for dirty cores
  - DirtyBin2: Bin 2 location for dirty cores
  - DirtyBin3: Bin 3 location for dirty cores
  - DirtyOnHand: Total of all the dirty cores in house
  - ExcessQty: Excess quantity
  - Exchange: Exchange or core price
  - ExtraDS: Extra days supply
  - FebSales: February demand history, current year
  - FebSales2: February demand history, last year
  - FebSales3: February demand history, two years ago
  - FullBin: Full bin; maximum stocking level for a part
  - GuaranteedQuantity: Guaranteed Quantity
  - HostItemID: Pick file item ID
  - JanSales: January demand history, current year
  - JanSales2: January demand history, last year
  - JanSales3: January demand history, two years ago
  - JulSales: July demand history, current year
  - JulSales2: July demand history, last year
  - JulSales3: July demand history, two years ago
  - JunSales: June demand history, current year
  - JunSales2: June demand history, last year
  - JunSales3: June demand history, two years ago
  - LastCountDate: Last date part was counted in physical inventory
  - LastSaleDate: Date of the last sale.
  - LastTransDate: Date of the last transaction
  - List: Retail price
  - Locked: Locked Flag
  - MFGControlled: MFG Controlled
  - MTDEmerPurchase: Emergency purchases this month
  - MTDLostSales: Lost sales this month
  - MTDMinusAdj: Minus adjustments this month
  - MTDPlusAdj: Plus adjustments this month
  - Manufacturer: Manufacturer code
  - MarSales: March demand history, current year
  - MarSales2: March demand history, last year
  - MarSales3: March demand history, two years ago
  - MaySales: May demand history, current year
  - MaySales2: May demand history, last year
  - MaySales3: May demand history, two years ago
  - MemoPartFlag: Memo Part Flag
  - Misc: Miscellaneous information needed by client
  - Month13Sales: Demand history for the current month one year ago
  - Month14Sales: Demand history for the prior month one year ago
  - MonthsNoReceipt: Number of consecutive months without receipt
  - MonthsNoSale: Number of consecutive months without sale
  - MonthsWithAtlestOneSale: Min No of months for a part to sell before it can be ordered for regular stocking
  - Multiple: The minimum quantity shipped by the manufacturer
  - NSRetentionPeriod: Number of months a part number with NS can remain in PART-No. file
  - NewOrderQty: New order quantity
  - NovSales: November demand history, current year
  - NovSales2: November demand history, last year
  - NovSales3: November demand history, two years ago
  - OTYPE: Order Type code.
  - OctSales: October demand history, current year
  - OctSales2: October demand history, last year
  - OctSales3: October demand history, two years ago
  - OldOnHand: Old on-hand quantity
  - OnHand: On-hand quantity
  - OnOrderQty: On-order quantity
  - PNC: Part number change
  - Pack: The number of pieces contained within a package
  - PackMultipleFlag: Package or multiple quantity flag
  - PartNumber: Part number
  - PerJob: Minimum on-hand quantity needed to complete a job
  - PreSoldQuantity: Pre Sold Quantity
  - PreviousPartNumber: Part number change
  - Price10: Extra pricing field #10
  - Price6: Extra pricing field #6
  - Price7: Extra pricing field #7
  - Price8: Extra pricing field #8
  - Price9: Extra pricing field #9
  - PriceUnit: Price unit
  - PriorYearSales1: Demand history for the prior year
  - PriorYearSales2: Demand history for two years ago
  - PriorYearSales3: Demand history for three years ago
  - QualMonthsForRegStockingStatus: Total month duration to check for regular stocking
  - RBCode: Supersession code
  - RequestedQuantity: Requested Quantity
  - Review: Review for quantity change
  - SLSTCNT: Last sales count date
  - SafetyStockLevel: The number that determines BSL
  - SeasonCode1: Seasonal code 1
  - SeasonCode2: Seasonal code 2
  - SeasonCode3: Seasonal code 3
  - SeasonCode4: Seasonal code 4
  - SeasonCode5: Seasonal code 5
  - SeasonCode6: Seasonal code 6
  - SepSales: September demand history, current year
  - SepSales2: September demand history, last year
  - SepSales3: September demand history, two years ago
  - SortKey1: Sort key 1 (Field5)
  - SortKey2: Sort key 2 (Field6)
  - SortKey3: Sort key 3 (Field7)
  - Source: Part source code
  - SpecialStatus: Special status
  - StraightLineAvgMonths: No of months to cal straight line average.
  - Trade: Trade or wholesale price
  - UnitWeight: Weight of each part in pounds or kilograms
  - UpdateCode: Update code from most recent manufacturer update
  - WebEnabled: Flag used by vendor, whether parts should be sold on web or not. Currently 1 or 0/null
  - YRSL: Total sales for last 12 months.

  - TechNo4: Technician number
  - TechNo5: Technician number

  - TimeCardHours: Number of timecard hours applied to the labor operation

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TABLE: VehicleTrans_v
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DESCRIPTION: Vehicle Transactions - Vehicle-related transactions.
FIELD COUNT: 17

FIELDS:
  - ElitePlusID: ElitePlus ID found in attribute 40 of CAR-INV and attribute 6 of VEHICLES. This attribute is only updated for CAR-INV and VEHICLES transactions.
  - FileType: The file type defines what file the unit transaction has affected.
  - HostItemID: The HostItemID is an ID generated by the EIP to uniquely identify how the record was generated.
  - ItemID: Item-ID of the file defined in FileType. The ID of the unit affected by the transaction.
  - LinkFileType: Filetype linked to filetype and item-ID associated with the transaction (attribute 1 and 2). This attribute is updated only for CAR-INV and VEHICLES records that link to each other.
  - LinkItemID: Item-ID linked to filetype and item-ID associated with the transaction (attribute 1 and 2). This attribute is updated only for CAR-INV and VEHICLES records that link to each other.
  - Message: Message text used when a message is displayed to the user.
  - NewData: Stores the new data value. Multi-valued and correlative to 9 & 11
  - OldData: Stores the data being changed. Multi-valued and correlative to 10 & 11
  - SystemDate: The ID is the current internal system date and the current system time (in milliseconds after midnight) when the transaction occurs. The date and time is concatenated with an asterisk '*' to form the ID.
  - SystemTime: The ID is the current internal system date and the current system time (in milliseconds after midnight) when the transaction occurs. The date and time is concatenated with an asterisk '*' to form the ID.
  - TransAcct: <OPTIONAL> Account from which the Transaction originated. For instance, ABC-FI
  - TransProcess: Process that initiated the transaction
  - TransRefer: <OPTIONAL> Reference number of the transaction. For instance, Deal#, G/L Reference #, RO#, etc.
  - TransType: The type of transaction.
  - UpdAttribute: Stores the updated attribute value. Multi-valued and correlative to 9 & 10
  - UserID: User ID for the process that initiated the transaction.

FIELDS:

  - SaleAmount: Retail sales price.
  - SatisfiedBy: Satisfied by.<P>Code for the DMS application that was used to satisfy the We Owe.
  - SatisfiedDate: Satisfied date.<P>Date the We Owe was satisfied by the dealership.
  - WeOweCode: We Owe code. A dealer-defined code set up for a We Owe.
  - WeOweDesc: We Owe description.<P>A dealer-defined description set up for a We Owe, or the description that is manually entered during the deal.

  - FormattedPartNumber: Manufacturer Part Format
  - HostItemID: OrderNumber * OrderDate * OrderType * OrderLine
  - ItemName: OrderNumber * OrderDate * OrderType * OrderLine
  - LastUpdate: When the order line was last modified
  - OemOrderNumber: OEM Order Number
  - OnHandQty: On hand quantity of part number
  - OrderDate: Order Date
  - OrderLine: Sequential line number
  - OrderNumber: Order Number
  - OrderPad: Order Pad
  - OrderQty: Quantity Ordered
  - OrderType: Order Type
  - OrderValue: Dollar value of the quantity ordered
  - PartDesc: Description of part number
  - PartNumber: Part number
  - PartNumberChangeFlag: Flag indicating order line transferred to PNC
  - ProcessFlag: Flag Indicating line is fully processed
  - ReceiptDate: When the order line was last receipted
  - ReceiptedQty: Quantity Receipted
  - Source: Source of part number
  - SpecialOrderBlankTypeFlag: Flag indicating SOR is blank type instead of U type
  - SpecialOrderFlag: Special order flag
  - SpecialStatus: Special status of part number
  - TransferQty: Quantity Transferred
